staging plan, 2024 and 2025
[
----- persons and cargo
acclimatization, scoping.
high safety margins, double capacity.
able to survive all four seasons, full year.


----- start staging -----
----- persons
10 million.
----- person trucks
20 million
----- cargo containers, 20,000 pound.
food = 2/person.
living = 2/person.
total = 40 million containers (10 million persons x 4).
----- cargo ships
1 ship = 100,000 containers.
400 ships = 400 x 100,000 = 40,000,000 million containers.
2,000,000 containers/month, 20 ships/month, 200 ships/year, 2 years.
On land and on ship storage.
----- person ships
1 ship = 2000 persons.
5,000 ships = 5,000 x 2,000 = 10,000,000 million persons.
500,000 persons/month, 250 ships/month, 2500 ships/year, 2 years.
On land and on board living.
----- person truck ships
1 ship = 50,000 person trucks.
400 ships = 400 x 50,000 = 20,000,000 million person trucks.
1,000,000 person trucks/month, 20 ships/month, 200 ships/year, 2 years.
On land and on ship storage.
----- end staging -----
]


landing plan, 2026
[
-----
here to stay.


----- start landing -----
----- ports and forts all along shore.
500 ports, 500 person ships, 500 cargo ships, 500 person truck ships and 500 forts.
----- person ships
500 forts, 2000 persons/fort = 1,000,000 million persons.
500 person ships x 2000 persons = 1,000,000 million persons.
1 ship/day, 30 ships/month, 60,000 persons/month, 350 ships/year, 1 year
Persons on land and on board.
----- cargo ships
1,000,000 persons x 4 containers/person = 4,000,000 containers.
500 cargo ships x 8,000 containers/ship = 4,000,000 containers.
1 ship/day, 30 ships/month, 240,000 containers/month, 350 ships/year, 1 year
Cargo on land and on board.
----- person truck ships
1,000,000 persons x 2 person trucks/person = 2,000,000 person trucks.
500 cargo ships x 4,000 person trucks/ship = 2,000,000 person trucks.
1 ships/day, 30 ships/month, 120,000 person trucks/month, 350 ships/year, 1 year
Cargo on land and on board.
----- end landing -----
]


offense plan, 2026
[
-----
ready to move interior


----- start offense -----
----- persons and equipment
100 ports x 1000 person/fort = 100,000 persons.
100 groups/fort x 10 person = 1,000 persons.
1,000 persons x 20 trucks = 20,000 person trucks/fort.
----- interior move - group size, persons and equipment
10 persons.
10 person trucks.
----- end offense -----
]

DSS Smart device and DSS Smart service


----- Open copyright, document, Rakesh Kukatla-Sittrue -----
DSS Smart device and DSS Smart service


DSS Smart device


Please make available DSS Smart devices (aka phone) at local broome county device retailers such as Best buy. At the present time these devices can only be procured via internet retail outlets.


DSS Smart service


Please make available DSS Smart service called data (aka plan) for the DSS Smart device at local broome county service retailers such as Verizon, ATT, Tmobile and Dish satellite. At the present time these plans can only be procured via internet retail outlets.


aka = also known as (in government language).
DSS = Department of Social Services
